  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0b5acffa-cbd3-4529-b949-e4f3e5bc57e6'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</script>

  <span id="freeText13603579148321792886" style="display:none"><b>Love is just around the corner . . . </b><br /><br />Sweet, shy Mara Hanover is in love with her neighbor. For four years, she has secretly watched her dream man from afar. Handsome police detective Mitch Lawson is way out of her league. She's a girl from the wrong side of the tracks, and there's no way a guy like Mitch would want anything to do with her. But when Mara has a leaky faucet that she can't fix, it's Mitch who comes to her rescue. <br /><br />Mitch has been eyeing his beautiful neighbor for a long time. He jumps at the chance to help her, and soon their formerly platonic relationship gets very hot and heavy. But when Mara gets a disturbing phone call from her cousin's kids, she gets pulled back into the life she's tried so hard to leave behind. Can the hot law man convince Mara to let go of her past-and build a future with him?</span>

<div id="review_279263085" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/279263085" />
    <a title="Mimi Smith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith"><img alt="Mimi Smith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1297016674p2/4884889.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/279263085?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mimi Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mimi Smith" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith">Mimi Smith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4884889-mimi-smith?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer279263085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6649292591300763354"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote><b>Dear Ms. Ashley</b><br/><br/>You probably don't know who I am, but pretty soon you will. Why, you ask yourself. Because I am going to kidnap Mitch Lawson and make him a part of my harem, of course. Now, I know nowadays harems aren't trendy, but as I was reading this book I realized I had a problem. There are just too many men I had already pledged to (including your fabulous heroes Brock and Ty), so I needed to think outside of the box. I realize having all those alpha men at the ready will be very c</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6649292591300763354" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br /><blockquote><b>Dear Ms. Ashley</b><br /><br />You probably don't know who I am, but pretty soon you will. Why, you ask yourself. Because I am going to kidnap Mitch Lawson and make him a part of my harem, of course. Now, I know nowadays harems aren't trendy, but as I was reading this book I realized I had a problem. There are just too many men I had already pledged to (including your fabulous heroes Brock and Ty), so I needed to think outside of the box. I realize having all those alpha men at the ready will be very challenging and a lifetime obligation. That's all right, I'm ready to work very, <i>very hard</i> at it. The moment I decided this was the only option was this...<br /><br /><i> “The man who gets Mara gets you and Billie. I’m that man. What you gotta get is, while fallin’ in love with Mara, I fell in love with you and your sister. Straight up, Bud, no lie. The feelings I feel for Mara are hers, the feelings I feel for Billie are hers and the feelings I feel for you are yours. You all have my love, not collectively, individually. Do you understand me?”<br /><br />"Mitch nodded. “Right. What I mean is, I didn’t fall in love with you all as a whole. I fell in love with each of you because of who you are. I don’t care about you because you come with Mara. I care about you because you’re a good kid. You’re smart. You’re loyal. And you love and look out for your sister and Mara. I know grown men who do not have a character as fine as yours. Those are the reasons I love you. There are different reasons I love Billie. And there are different reasons I love Mara. Today, what we had together was good. But the feelings I feel for you aren’t feelings I have to have in order to have Mara. They’re feelings you earned. Now, you with me?”</i><br /><br />If this letter fell accidentally, in hands of someone who doesn't know who Billy, Billie and Mara are, let me explain.<br /><br />Mara is the totally undeserving girlfriend of Mitch. I know, I know-I shouldn't say something like that, especially after the hard life she had, but as Mitch said...<br /><br /><i>"I was right. Your head is right up your ass."</i><br /><br />That girl needs therapy. The point system idea is so whacked. Who lives their life by devising a point system where every person has a certain value, based on their looks, and upon further knowledge, attitude and is then judged by that? Don't understand, here's an example...<br /><br /><i>"His mother was probably a Ten Point Five too and Ten Point Fives didn’t help out Two Point Fives."</i><br /><br />That's so wrong, it's not even funny. What, now an attractive person can't help out a person who isn't as attractive? Ms. Ashley, why on Earth did you write something like that? I know, later I was supposed to see how she got over that with the help of Mitch and the kids, but she never redeemed herself completely for me. That's why this Mitch-napping is also for his own good. He'll be happier this way.<br /><br />While we're here exchanging words, I have a request to make. Would you please consider writing a kick-ass, strong, confident heroine for a change. Not a clumsy, self conscious, low self esteem one. Because, no matter how much I like Tack, I don't want to be forced to take him in for his own good, too. Plus, I'd like to see a woman like that with him. It would definitely take him down a peg or two. Maybe she could be a detective? Now that's a storyline that would totally rock.<br /><br />Now, where was I....Oh, yeah. Billy and Billie. I'm still incredulous about those names. I think even you mixed them up from time to time. Billy's the boy and Billie's the girl which Mara and Mitch took in, after their father (you've guessed it) Bill (who is Mara's cousin, the scumbag) gets himself in jail. Billy and Billie are like the cutest kids ever. Don't worry about them. I'll totally adopt them when I get Mitch. <br /><br /><i>"I decided to shift the subject and asked gently, “You sleep okay, sweetie?”<br />“Miss my teddy,” Billie replied.<br />Personally, I thought Detective Mitch Lawson was far superior to a tiny pink teddy bear but I wasn’t six years old."</i><br /><br />Far superior, but the kids are cute. That speech at the beginning, those are Mitch's words to Billy, explaining his love for them. Didn't I say he was perfect.<br /><br />That was all I meant to say, but I thought it was fair to mention the good stuff about their relationship, as well. Even though it totally defies my purpose...<br /><br /><u>Her infatuation...</u><br /><br /><i>"I was in love with him and I didn’t know him and he definitely didn’t know me. This was not in a sick-stalker-type way because I was too shy to be a stalker and I liked him too much to put him through something like that. This was in an ohmigod he’s got the perfect body, perfect bone structure, perfect smile, most beautiful eyes I’ve ever seen way. It was totally benign, admiring from afar except that we lived across and one down the breezeway from each other so it wasn’t that far."</i><br /><br /><u>Their arguments...</u><br /><br /><i>…my eyes slid to Mitch whereupon I engaged my retinal laser beam to target Mitch who was not supposed to be sprawled on my couch eating donuts with the kids before nine o’clock. In fact, he was not supposed to be in my house at all until eleven o’clock. Unfortunately, my retinal laser beam malfunctioned and Mitch wasn’t incinerated.</i><br /><br /><u>Him explaining she has to see the light...</u><br /><br /><i>“Mara,” his arms gave me a squeeze, “baby, you’ve got to live in the now. Not in your head. Not controlled by your fears. You can’t live for what might happen five months in the future. You got issues you gotta face today. You gotta deal with them now. You got two kids who count on you and their lives aren’t gonna go perfect every day because you weigh every decision you make and tread cautiously. Those options are no longer available to you. You’re gonna have to live day to day and make decisions on the fly. And I’m tellin’ you I’m here to help. You need it and they need it. Are you honestly gonna say no?”</i><br /><br /><u>And her FINALLY seeing it...</u><br /><br /><i>"I didn’t need it.<br />Because I wasn’t a Two Point Five. I wasn’t an Eight. I wasn’t a Ten.<br />Mitch was right. My classification system was bullshit.<br />Bottom line, what I was is a decent person."</i><br /><br />I hate being fair. I totally feel like pouting right now... <br /><br />All in all, I'm just telling you to be prepared for imminent events. If you want to bribe me to stop, write me in with Tack. WITH Tack, you know? *waggles eyebrows*<br /><br /><b>Love Mimi</b><br /><br />P.S. If my plans are derailed, please do put Mara in therapy. At least for a while. Those kind of delusions don't just go away. Thanks! <br /><br /> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/277975880" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 1 in the series</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/278771417" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 2 in the series</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/336327385" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 4 in the series</a></blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="6649292591300763354" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3501049592" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3501049592" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3501049592?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3501049592" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2268833346836235670"><b>[2nd Read]</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1604151008i/30314325._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Oct. 2020 — 5 Stars</b><br/><br/>YES I RE-READ IT FRONT TO BACK TOP TO BOTTOM. FORGET EVERYTHING I SAID, ANY CRITICISM AND WHATNOT, CUZ I . . . LIKE IT, LOVE IT, LICK IT, DO IT LIKE LA LA LA OH YEAH. (Whoops that’s Blackpink, <i>Ice Cream</i>. Please ignore me cause that’s lame and you know it. 🙈)<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1604151008i/30314326._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>[1st Read]<br/><br/>Aug. 2020 — 4.25 Stars </b><br/><br/>What is it about KA’s books that you can’t help but love? I’ve only read two of her books. It could be my luck (if so, I hope it never runs out), and it might be too early to gener</span>
  <span id="freeText2268833346836235670" style="display:none"><b>[2nd Read]</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1604151008i/30314325._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Oct. 2020 — 5 Stars</b><br><br>YES I RE-READ IT FRONT TO BACK TOP TO BOTTOM. FORGET EVERYTHING I SAID, ANY CRITICISM AND WHATNOT, CUZ I . . . LIKE IT, LOVE IT, LICK IT, DO IT LIKE LA LA LA OH YEAH. (Whoops that’s Blackpink, <i>Ice Cream</i>. Please ignore me cause that’s lame and you know it. 🙈)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1604151008i/30314326._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>[1st Read]<br><br>Aug. 2020 — 4.25 Stars </b><br><br>What is it about KA’s books that you can’t help but love? I’ve only read two of her books. It could be my luck (if so, I hope it never runs out), and it might be too early to generalise her brilliance, but <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_" title="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a>
</i> was a win. It wasn’t smooth sailing, but I ended up loving it nonetheless.<br><br><blockquote>
<b>Mara</b> is shy and in love with her 10.5 neighbor. For some f*cked up reason, she got it branded in her brain that she’s a 2.5; and thus, WAY out of his league. Unbeknownst to her, detective <b>Mitch</b> has been harboring a crush of his own. So when a chance at encounter in the form of Mara’s leaky faucet greets him, he quickly jumps at the opportunity.</blockquote><br>(✗) <b>
  <u>The <s>awful</s> writing</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>1. <i>Hot, hot, hot</i><br>2. <i>Belly whoosh, another belly whoosh</i><br>3. <i>Nice, great, beautiful, gorgeous</i><br>4. Something about Mitch’s eyes.<br>5. Shoot, I should’ve made a list to give you more proof!</blockquote><br>I didn’t notice it the first time because I was too busy drooling over Kah Lahn (<i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12458287.The_Golden_Dynasty__Fantasyland___2_" title="The Golden Dynasty (Fantasyland, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">The Golden Dynasty</a>
</i>), but I caught on to KA’s HIGH tendency to repeat words, phrases, and use run on sentences. I mean, Idk if this style was intentional or not, but it certainly grated on my nerves. Like, she’s written dozens of books each with 500+ pages. Yet her vocabulary seems to have never improved.<br><br>(✗) <b>
  <u>The thick skulled h</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Ones to Threes gravitated to each other. If you were of my zone, only the foolish aimed higher than a Three. Higher than a Three equaled heartache.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Lemme tell you straight, Mara is one of the most frustrating heroines I’ve ever met and she didn’t deserve Mitch for the first 2/3 of the book. She constantly beats herself up and truly believes she’s unattractive even when her friends tell her otherwise. She also doesn’t know how to speak, except to utter the words “what?” and “pardon?” Her cluelessness was cute for a while, but it got old when she couldn’t get her head out of her ass fast enough. IT WAS <s>F*CKING</s> EXHAUSTING!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I didn’t need it. Because I wasn’t a Two Point Five. I wasn’t an Eight. I wasn’t a Ten. Mitch was right. My classification system was bullshit. Bottom line, what I was is a decent person.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>It’s like she’s been brainwashed or was a victim of some cults or something. (Actually, it’s because of her traumatic childhood.) She badly needs therapy, but all I wanted to do was shake her and slap her into next week. HOWEVER, (thank goodness for character development!) when she finally opens her eyes and stands up to her horrible mother, she’s AMAZING. I was cheering her on like a proud mama. Apart from all that, I loved how nice and kind she was with her friends, neighbors, and coworkers.<br><br>(✓) <b>
  <u>The dreamy H</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ll go gentle, baby,” he whispered against my lips. “I promise. You’ll always be safe with me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I think the answer to my initial question earlier is <b>MITCHELL JAMES LAWSON</b>. Idk if writing the perfect H is KA’s specialty, but so far two of her Hs have completely swept me off my feet . . .<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597692966ra/29980533.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>God, I LOVE Mitch so much I wanna weep. 😭 He’s so attentive, accomodating, patient, sexy, sweet, caring, protective, and reliable. He says and do the right things. Also, have I told you that I have a thing for law enforcement officers or men in uniforms (e.g. PILOTS, cops, etc.)?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The huddle included Slim, Tack, Delgado and a local private investigator, Hank Nightingale’s brother, Lee Nightingale and Lee’s second in command, Luke Stark.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>We met other Hs from the rest of the series in this book, and from those cameos, let’s just say that KA got it right when she named them <i>Dream Men</i>. I’m not sure I’ll pick up their books anytime soon, but I’m all ears if you wanna try to convince me.<br><br>(✓) <b>
  <u>Billy and Billie</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
    <b>
      <i>“Right. What I mean is, I didn’t fall in love with you all as a whole. I fell in love with each of you because of who you are. I don’t care about you because you come with Mara. I care about you because you’re a good kid. You’re smart. You’re loyal. And you love and look out for your sister and Mara. I know grown men who do not have a character as fine as yours. Those are the reasons I love you. There are different reasons I love Billie. And there are different reasons I love Mara. Today, what we had together was good. But the feelings I feel for you aren’t feelings I have to have in order to have Mara. They’re feelings you earned. Now, you with me?”</i>
    </b>
   <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</blockquote><br>Need I say more? These kids are wonderful. Sometimes I couldn’t tell them apart cause their names were pronounced the same and I was listening on audio. Regardless, every single moment with them was precious. The <i>Men Don’t Have Moments</i> chapter is one of my favorites. 😭<br><br>(✓) <b>
  <u>The romance &amp; suspense</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Let’s see if I can tear that cocoon wide open and let my Mara fly.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>At one point, I was so baffled by what a nut Mara was. She’s freaking unbelievable. I thought, what is a man like Mitch doing with her?! On the other hand, I loved that Mitch never gave up on Mara despite her stubborness and low self esteem. He’s always so understanding and persistent but never forceful.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No, I was made to protect you, and you were made in a way that it would always be worth the effort.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I ate up their budding romance! From being neighbors, to friends, to co-parenting, to roomates, and lovers. It’s not exactly the slowburn with sexually charged tension, but it’s the deep, beautiful, and emotional kind.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“That’s me,” Tack answered. “Full of surprises. Now, you gonna give Lawson his assurances and make your call or are we gonna get out our knitting needles and chat while we make scarves.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The suspense plotline eventually kicks in during the last 1/3. I was instantly HOOKED. I loved the twists and turns, the danger and action sequences. It gives the book more spice. Honestly, for most of the first half, I was ready to hand in a three stars, but it ultimately got better and even made me cry a few tears.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1604151168i/30314340._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In short, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_" title="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a>
</i> was addictive. It left me hungover and overwhelmed with feelings. And this quote, <i>“you were made in a way that it would always be worth the effort,”</i> also applied to me and this book cause despite my reservations about the writing and the h; Mitch, the kids, and everything else made all the fuss worth it.<br><br><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2268833346836235670" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_381179554" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/381179554" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/381179554?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781478954781" href="/book/show/18949569-law-man">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer381179554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13453476141212457334"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/9cbd5f90-a213-4cc4-9285-18303dd11c1d_zpsa3180d61.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387671081i/7648038.jpg' alt=' photo 9cbd5f90-a213-4cc4-9285-18303dd11c1d_zpsa3180d61.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Mitch Lawson may be the dreamiest of the dream men! He wasn’t quite as alpha as Hawk, Tack, or Brock, but he was so damn sweet, loving and kind and that made him super sexy! <br/><br/>Mara comes from trash. She doesn’t communicate with most of her family, except her cousin Bill and his two kids. She left that life 13 years ago and she’s never going back. But the life she grew up living took its toll. She has low self esteem, and even though she’s made something of herself, has great friends,</span>
  <span id="freeText13453476141212457334" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/9cbd5f90-a213-4cc4-9285-18303dd11c1d_zpsa3180d61.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387671081i/7648038.jpg" alt=" photo 9cbd5f90-a213-4cc4-9285-18303dd11c1d_zpsa3180d61.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mitch Lawson may be the dreamiest of the dream men! He wasn’t quite as alpha as Hawk, Tack, or Brock, but he was so damn sweet, loving and kind and that made him super sexy! <br><br>Mara comes from trash. She doesn’t communicate with most of her family, except her cousin Bill and his two kids. She left that life 13 years ago and she’s never going back. But the life she grew up living took its toll. She has low self esteem, and even though she’s made something of herself, has great friends, a good job, and a nice place, she never feels good enough. <br><br>Her neighbor and crush, Detective Mitch Lawson is a solid 10.5 and way out of her league. That hasn’t stopped her from wanting him the last few years. One day, Mara’s faucet is running and she asks her neighbors to help her fix it. Mitch over hears and offers his services. They click. It appears Mitch is into Mara just as she is into him, but she has trouble believing this. <br><br>Mara has a lot going on in her life. When her cousin gets into trouble, and she becomes guardian to his precious children, Billy and Billie, Mitch is there every step of the way to help her out. He wants to be there for her, for the kids. He’s all in. It just takes Mara a long time to realize this. To make her realize she is good enough, and Mitch does want her, he has his work cut out for him.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/48bbfdb7-1f6d-470a-b759-7c48e8f99bed_zps4c683efd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387671081i/7648039.jpg" alt=" photo 48bbfdb7-1f6d-470a-b759-7c48e8f99bed_zps4c683efd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mitch was AMAZING! The kids were AMAZING! Mara was a little annoying, but amazing at times (she doesn’t get the caps). Mitch won me over with his talk with Billy. I’ve never swooned so hard...<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“What I mean is, I didn't fall in love with you all as a whole. I fell in love with each of you because of who you are. I don't care about you because you come with Mara. I care about you because you're a good kid. You're smart. You're loyal. And you love and look out for your sister and Mara. I know grown men who do not have a character as fine as yours. Those are the reasons I love you. There are different reasons I love Billie. And there are different reasons I love Mara. Today, what we had together was good. But the feelings I feel for you aren't feelings I have to have in order to have Mara. They're feelings you earned. Now, you with me?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> Then he also says stuff like this... How can you not love this man???<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I'll go gentle, baby," he whispered against my lips. "I promise. You'll always be safe with me."<br>Oh. My.<br>"Mitch," I breathed.<br>His soulful eyes held mine captive as he repeated firmly, "Always.” <br><br>“That's another thing that doesn't turn me off, sweetheart, knowin' that you come with those kids and you need to know that. You also need to know I want kids of my own, two of them. But I don't care, if this works out between me and you, that the kids we have will have an older brother and sister that don't have my blood, just my heart.” <br><br>“You're Mara, you're sweet, you're beautiful and I will not forget until the day I die how beautiful it felt to slide inside you with you wrapped around me, see your eyes get wet and know straight in my gut that you felt how beautiful it was too.” </blockquote>
</i> Just a random- I listened to this audiobook and I’m just going to note that the Billy/Billie thing was really confusing for me. When you can’t see how it’s spelled and they are randomly saying Billy/Billie all the time it throws you off. I was never so happy then when Mitch started calling Billy, Bud!<br><br>Law Man was awesome! Mitch and Mara were great. It was nice to catch up with Hawk, Tack, Brock and the rest of the gang. How much did I like this book? In true Kristen Ashley fashion, I’ll say a fuckovalot! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/dfaad50a-da52-4f7e-9c1f-0abe2865a111_zpsdcb3ab94.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387671081i/7648040.jpg" alt=" photo dfaad50a-da52-4f7e-9c1f-0abe2865a111_zpsdcb3ab94.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13453476141212457334" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/626523971?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18888391-law-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=indie">indie</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=the-heart-wants-what-the">the-heart-wants-what-the</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=buddy-reads-are-the-best">buddy-reads-are-the-best</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer626523971" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer108903815151824953"><b>4.0 HAWT Alpha Good Guy stars</b><br/><br/>I love Mitch. <br/><br/>There I said it. I love him, and I don't care if other KA fangirls think he's boring, I think he's awesome:<br/><br/>1. He's a COP. That's always hot.<br/>2. He took on Mara despite her being a HEADCASE, and despite her suddenly deciding to take on guardianship for two small children.<br/><br/>Actually, that's why I love it right there. <br/><br/>Once upon a time, I was one of those kids, and I had my own Mitch. <br/><br/>Then I grew up to marry another Mitch. <br/><br/>Kind of. He's an engineer, not a cop,</span>
  <span id="freeText108903815151824953" style="display:none"><b>4.0 HAWT Alpha Good Guy stars</b><br><br>I love Mitch. <br><br>There I said it. I love him, and I don't care if other KA fangirls think he's boring, I think he's awesome:<br><br>1. He's a COP. That's always hot.<br>2. He took on Mara despite her being a HEADCASE, and despite her suddenly deciding to take on guardianship for two small children.<br><br>Actually, that's why I love it right there. <br><br>Once upon a time, I was one of those kids, and I had my own Mitch. <br><br>Then I grew up to marry another Mitch. <br><br>Kind of. He's an engineer, not a cop, and I was sans children, but still, everyone who knows us agrees that I married a carbon copy of my dad (&lt;------he gave my sister and me his name, too). <br><br>So there's really no way I wouldn't have loved this one. <br><br>Then there's Mara, and I'll admit, she takes a little getting used to. She's one of KA's more neurotic heroines, but the more time you spend with her, the more sympathetic you become, and by the end, you love her as much as Mitch, b/c dollface is STRONG. <br><br>And good. And determined. And she loves those kids so damn much.<br><br>What kids?<br><br>Billy and Billie, her second cousins by way of her cousin Bill (who, YES, is an assclown who named BOTH his kids after his assclown-self).<br><br>Not only did this cheesehead name his daughter Billerina, he also spends his questionably acquired income on drugs and alcohol, which he uses without regard to any tiny people who are present.<br><br>Not food. Not clothes. Not basic necessities for his two children. <br><br>So Mara(belle &lt;------how pretty is that), steps up, making the decision she'd been grappling with for awhile, and starts pursuing custody of them.<br><br>And Mitch doesn't leave her side for a second. Well, okay, he does once, but only for a few days, and then he's comes back and refuses to be pushed out again.<br><br>I want all KA heroines and Alphas to get their HEAs, but these guys are up there with Joe, Violet, and her girls (from 'THE BURG #2). <br><br>ALSO, there are more cameos from ROCK CHICK than I remember seeing anywhere else, and that includes a scene with Lee Nightingale, Hank Nightingale, and LUKE STARK all in the same room together.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411926476ra/11300873.gif" width="380" height="186" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So yeah, LAW MAN . . . you should read it. <br><br><b>11/15/15:</b> As <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14105531" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Robin</a>
</b> said, the KA Buddy (Re)Read madness continues with <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14323468" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Joanita</a>
</b>, <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/10037544" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Stephanie</a>
</b> and <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/27962805" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Choko</a>
</b> over at <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">BB&amp;B</a>
</b>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446128036i/16751969.jpg" width="255" height="361" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>B/c KA. #cantstopwontstop</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1390101195" />
    <a title="Mysza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza"><img alt="Mysza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433922560p2/14262653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1390101195?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mysza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mysza" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza">Mysza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1390101195" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15633208785836241222">It kills me to write this review because after being on a roll with KA books and loving all of them, this is the first one that didn't impress me. Don't get me wrong, the story was good, Mitch Lawson was KA's usual badass, the other characters were great too, and I was glad to see the ones from other books make an appearance. But when the highlight of the book is when my man Hawk or my dearest biker Tack shows up, then there's definitely something wrong with the book for me. <br/><br/>The main reason woul</span>
  <span id="freeText15633208785836241222" style="display:none">It kills me to write this review because after being on a roll with KA books and loving all of them, this is the first one that didn't impress me. Don't get me wrong, the story was good, Mitch Lawson was KA's usual badass, the other characters were great too, and I was glad to see the ones from other books make an appearance. But when the highlight of the book is when my man Hawk or my dearest biker Tack shows up, then there's definitely something wrong with the book for me. <br /><br />The main reason would be the heroine Mara, who was simply getting on my nerves with her "two point five" evaluation system. The phrases she used the most were: "I...", "Uhm...", "Mitch...". At some point I was surprised she was able to utter something more than this. She finally grew some balls but it was too little too late for me. <br /><br />I'm just sad because I'm sure if Mitch was paired with a stronger heroine, his story could have been so much better. That being said, it was the least favourite in the series for me, with Hawk and Tack's books staying my top favourites.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15633208785836241222" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of emotional contemporary romance &amp; unforgettable heroes</span></div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer268036773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6427433273460403345">5+ stars – Contemporary Romance<br/><br/><i>GAWD</i> I loved this book so much! There are many things that make this a great read but the reasons can be easily summarized in three words repeated over and over again: Detective Mitch Lawson. A <i>
  <b>Law Man</b>
</i> and <i>Dream Man</i> extraordinaire, he is without a doubt my favorite Kristen Ashley alpha hero and one of the most swoonalicious, studtastic, heart thud inducing, and sigh-worthy heroes in Romancelandia. Seriously, Mitch is yummy husband hero material and utterly amaz</span>
  <span id="freeText6427433273460403345" style="display:none">5+ stars – Contemporary Romance<br><br><i>GAWD</i> I loved this book so much! There are many things that make this a great read but the reasons can be easily summarized in three words repeated over and over again: Detective Mitch Lawson. A <i>
  <b>Law Man</b>
</i> and <i>Dream Man</i> extraordinaire, he is without a doubt my favorite Kristen Ashley alpha hero and one of the most swoonalicious, studtastic, heart thud inducing, and sigh-worthy heroes in Romancelandia. Seriously, Mitch is yummy husband hero material and utterly amazing in every single way and then some.<br><br>I’ll be honest that I wanted to smack Mara silly for about the first 30+% of the book. Her constant judging and referring to people in terms of their zone number...“they’re a 7.5, I’m a 2.5, and he’s a 10.5”...really annoyed me. There were times when I wondered, why doesn’t Mitch ever let Mara talk or even finish a freaking sentence? (This is a common behavior with all of Kristen Ashley’s alpha heroes.) But then I was like, oh wait, maybe it’s because all she ever says is “uh...”, “um...”, “pardon me?”, and “sorry?”! And I found myself agreeing with Mitch’s harsh assessment that Mara seriously needed to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[get her head out of her ass <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. But once Mara’s past was revealed and her batsh*t crazy relatives came calling; I understood and liked her much better. And I was so proud of her along with Mitch when she finally recognized her own self worth, found some backbone, and stood up for herself and <i>her</i> kids.<br><br>That brings me to another main reason I loved this book so much, which is the adorable, heartstring-tugging kids, Billy/Bud and Billie, and the cute, sweet, and emotional moments between them, Mara, and Mitch. There were several poignant scenes that choked me up and had tears streaming down my cheeks and others that brought a big smile to my face.<br><br>Like all of the previous Kristen Ashley books that I’ve read, this grabbed me from the very beginning, kept me engaged throughout, and had me anxiously yearning for a HEA finale. And once again, like all of KA’s stories, I was sad for it to end and grateful for the beautiful, touching epilogue that is in and of itself worthy of 5+ stars. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The scene in the epilogue where Bud pounds a fist over his heart while staring meaningfully at Mitch on his way to the baseball dugout had me gulping back sobs. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And the romance? Oh yeah! It’s intense, sexy, and smokin’ <i>hot</i>! <i>
  <b>Law Man</b>
</i> is another Kristen Ashley winner! Big 5 stars!<br><br>Josh Duhamel is my Detective Mitch Lawson, and he definitely has the soulful brown eyes. <i>*sigh*</i><br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=BBC-023440.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380368329i/720891._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_887902740" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/887902740" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/887902740?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer887902740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17414793894181579727"><b>Re-read July 2015</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437579734i/15599579.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>"I'm thinkin' I fell in love with the promise of you the first time I saw you.”-Mitch</b><br/><br/>Every time I pick up a Kristen Ashley book it is like coming home. For me, she has the ability to sweep me away into another world. I find assurance that I will experience the joy of meeting a new "Alpha Male" and a heroine with some sort of quirk. Although Ms. Ashley's dialogue and style is unique, I am never deterred from spending hours upon hours reading and re-reading her work. She puts a s</span>
  <span id="freeText17414793894181579727" style="display:none"><b>Re-read July 2015</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437579734i/15599579.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"I'm thinkin' I fell in love with the promise of you the first time I saw you.”-Mitch</b><br><br>Every time I pick up a Kristen Ashley book it is like coming home. For me, she has the ability to sweep me away into another world. I find assurance that I will experience the joy of meeting a new "Alpha Male" and a heroine with some sort of quirk. Although Ms. Ashley's dialogue and style is unique, I am never deterred from spending hours upon hours reading and re-reading her work. She puts a smile on my face every time! Law Man is the third book in the Dream Man Series. This was the first KA series that I read and it has been a real treat to come back and re-acclimate myself with these men and their crazy women!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437587441i/15600250._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>"It was my experience if something bad could happen, it would, and I was always planning for that day."- Mara</b><br><br>In Law Man we find Mara a shy and slightly broken young woman. She has escaped the trailer park of her past and been successful making a life for herself in Colorado. Mara is a likable character however, she certainly has her issues. Although it is quite understandable for her to struggle with her self confidence, at times it could be a bit tedious with her constant need to "rank" herself and the others around her. She sees herself as someone unworthy of happiness and true greatness.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437579734i/15599580._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Lucky for Mara, the answer to her self doubting and fears lives right across the breezeway. Mitch Lawson is a private detective and exudes hotness. Mara has always had a thing for the attractive detective, and yet she can barely make eye contact with the man. When Mara needs help with a broken pipe in her apartment, Mitch comes in to save the day. The two quickly have a connection and Mitch makes it his mission to win over Mara.<br><br><b>“Let's see if I can tear that cocoon wide open and let my Mara fly.”-Mitch</b><br><br>Before Mitch and Mara have the opportunity to form a stable friendship/relationship, Mara's two younger cousins enter the picture. They are in need of help and Mara and Mitch together bring them home and give them love and attention. While loving on these two beautiful kids, Mitch makes a break through with Mara and she begins to experience real love for the first time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437587207i/15600216.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>“The man who gets Mara gets you and Billie. I’m that man. What you gotta get is, while fallin’ in love with Mara, I fell in love with you and your sister. Straight up, Bud, no lie. The feelings I feel for Mara are hers, the feelings I feel for Billie are hers and the feelings I feel for you are yours. You all have my love, not collectively, individually. Do you understand me?” -Mitch</b><br><br>The journey the four of them make together is beautiful. There are so many tender moments and points in the timeline where I couldn't help but feel warm and fuzzy all over. The steam factor is in true KA fashion "OFF THE CHARTS"! Mitch and Mara are a more gentle couple compared to other racey KA characters. However, I found the pairing perfect and delightful to read. The struggles in this book are centered on self esteem, overcoming abuse, and finding peace. I truly enjoyed the added element of "the blended family". Sometimes adding children to a book can be distracting from the romance element, and yet I found that the addition of these two sweet kids only strengthened my love for Mitch and Mara.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437582444i/15599827.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Overall, another winner for me! If you are a fan of Kristen Ashely, I highly recommend this book and the entire series. There are always references to other characters from other books as they weave in and out of the action. The character development is flawless and full of life. I look forward to reading a Kristen Ashely book for the first time but sometimes reading it the second time around makes it that much sweeter! <br><br><b><br>“Thank you, honey,” she kept whispering.<br>“For what?”<br>“A good life and a beautiful family.”<br>“You had a hand in that,” he reminded her.<br>“I know. We’re a team. Thank you for giving me that too.” </b><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><b>Original read- March 21,2014</b><br>Mitch and Mara's love story is one of my new faves! Fun read!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17414793894181579727" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/272283483?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=favorite-hero">favorite-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer272283483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14824893418211996416"><b>5+ stars</b><br/><br/><b>Full review posted. Finally!</b><br/><br/>Fantastic! I loved this book. Kristen Ashley created magic when she brought to life this heartfelt story and the amazingly swoonalicious hero, Mitch Lawson. <br/><br/>This book is chock-full of heart-and-soul. It has an emotional subject matter, humor, suspense, steamy romance, and very endearing characters. Well, Mara, the heroine, did annoy me for a portion of the book with her insecurity. I understand why she had such low self-worth, but I came to love her once she r</span>
  <span id="freeText14824893418211996416" style="display:none"><b>5+ stars</b><br /><br /><b>Full review posted. Finally!</b><br /><br />Fantastic! I loved this book. Kristen Ashley created magic when she brought to life this heartfelt story and the amazingly swoonalicious hero, Mitch Lawson. <br /><br />This book is chock-full of heart-and-soul. It has an emotional subject matter, humor, suspense, steamy romance, and very endearing characters. Well, Mara, the heroine, did annoy me for a portion of the book with her insecurity. I understand why she had such low self-worth, but I came to love her once she realized the error in her thinking. <br /><br />Now for Mitch! Oh my, how I love him! I can't rave about his character enough. I simply fell head-over-heels for him. I believe he's the perfect combination of all Kristen Ashley's heroes, making him practically perfect in every way. He is definitely my favorite Kristen Ashley hero to date. I just adore him!<br /><br />My favorite part of this book is the relationship that develops between Mitch, Mara, and two children–Billy a boy, and Billie a girl, who are the children of Mara's cousin Bill. Yes, their drug addict father gave them both the same name, just with different spellings. Mara ends up gaining custody of the children, and thus begins the heartwarming story about a family in the making. <br /><br />The quote below sums up this book and shows why Mitch Lawson is my favorite Kristen Ashley hero. <br /><br /><i>“The man who gets Mara gets you and Billie. I’m that man. What you gotta get is, while fallin’ in love with Mara, I fell in love with you and your sister. Straight up, Bud, no lie. The feelings I feel for Mara are hers, the feelings I feel for Billie are hers and the feelings I feel for you are yours. You all have my love, not collectively, individually. Do you understand me?” </i><br /><br />Once again Kristen Ashley dazzled me with her storytelling ability and her feel-good epilogues. This book's epilogue left me with a warm heart and tears in my eyes. No one write epilogues like Ashley. I highly recommend this book. <br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14824893418211996416" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText13910508492421088585" style="display:none"><br /><b>Ooooh! Kristen Ashley's LAW MAN is a Kindle Daily Deal - 1/3/2014 - just $0.99!! </b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00AHFJACW?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=213733&amp;creative=393177&amp;creativeASIN=B00AHFJACW&amp;linkCode=shr&amp;tag=blitbookrevi-20&amp;SIN=B00AHFJACW">http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00A...</a> <br /><br />Awesome, funny, sexy, poignant, exciting, sexy, awesome, sexy… <i>Law Man</i>, the third book in the <i>Dream Man</i> series is all kinds of greatness! Mitch Lawson is one of my absolute favorite KA heroes and I just adored Mara! She might be shy, but she’s no Shrinking Violet!!! <br /><br />Besides the suspense of the story plot, there’s the sadness that comes with child neglect, and then the joy that comes from belonging to a family who chooses you, wants you, loves you… Kristen Ashley did a great job tackling some tough, emotion issues. And if seeing them get their <i>happily ever after</i> then and there isn't enough for you, the epilogue, which takes place years in the future, is wonderful!!!<br /><br />One of my very favorite things about this story is when Mara’s mother and Aunt Lulamae come on scene… those ladies are some crazy ass bitches, and I don’t mean that in a good way. There’s a reason they’re called The Trailer Trash Twins, and maybe it was wrong for me to laugh so hard at them, but damn, I couldn’t help it!!<br /><br />Anyway, another great installment of the <i>Dream Man</i> series and I’m SOOO looking forward to reading Tack’s story in <i>Motorcycle Man</i>.<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! <br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1705360637" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10465106799092628519"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 7/23/2016)</i></b><br/><br/><b>3.5 Stars<i>* (Re-Read 5/31/2018)</i></b><br/><br/><b>3.5 Stars<i>** (Re-Read 4/4/2020)</i></b><br/><br/><b>*Re-Read note:</b>. It was still an enjoyable read. I loved the H with the kids again, and the epilogue was awesome! However, the h getting bulldozed by the H so easily bugged me in this for some reason this time reading it. Yes, that's typical KA interactions -- BUT it made me want to scream "quit interrupting her, and listen!!" a few times. Her insecurities also bugged. Hence, the reason for my drop in </span>
  <span id="freeText10465106799092628519" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 7/23/2016)</i></b><br /><br /><b>3.5 Stars<i>* (Re-Read 5/31/2018)</i></b><br /><br /><b>3.5 Stars<i>** (Re-Read 4/4/2020)</i></b><br /><br /><b>*Re-Read note:</b>. It was still an enjoyable read. I loved the H with the kids again, and the epilogue was awesome! However, the h getting bulldozed by the H so easily bugged me in this for some reason this time reading it. Yes, that's typical KA interactions -- BUT it made me want to scream "quit interrupting her, and listen!!" a few times. Her insecurities also bugged. Hence, the reason for my drop in rating after the re-read.<br /><br /><b>**Re-Read note:</b> Not much to add here. I'm keeping my rating the same. I still enjoyed the interactions with the kids, found the h's insecurities a little annoying, and enjoyed their HEA. Overall, still good for a re-read!<br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was pretty much cookie cutter Kristen Ashley. It had the typical type of characters, formatting, and even some of the dialogue that some people hate was here as well (the h saying things like "pardon", "um", "what" when being bulldozed by the H). Did that bother me at all? No! I like cookie cutter KA! I don't mind that it was similar to some of her other books because of those things, because it works for me. I enjoy these books. I like books with mcs that have interactions with kids, and KA is a go-to author when I'm wanting that type of storyline. Did I love it? No. But I did like it. It made me smile and feel good at the end. :)<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Mara and Mitch's story. They have been neighbors for ~4 years when Mitch offers to help Mara with a faulty faucet. Some unfortunate events occur, and Mara finds herself responsible for her cousin's 2 children. At this point, Mitch has planted himself into Mara's life and is insistent that he will help her with her big life change. There is some family drama, some sexy and sweet times, and some suspenseful moments...but they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was mostly told in Mara's POV, but a few sections were in Mitch's.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. Typical KA formatting (long, lots of details, and dramatic conflict at end to be resolved with a HEA). It flowed well, and I never skimmed.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. They both had been acquaintances for ~4 years, and both had been attracted to each other and never did anything about it. They started with some feelings already there, but I wouldn't call it instalove.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Mitch. He was an alpha, pushy, sometime a jerk, but also really sweet...a typical KA hero.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Mara. She was a super sweet, loving, insecure but shouldn't be...a typical KA heroine.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low. No tissues required.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H pursues the h. She is hesitant for a while and pushes him away, but he is persistent and eventually gets through to her.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. They have some good chemistry and scenes.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b>Yes. Condoms and birth control are mentioned. I don't remember any mention of past practices. <br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Very minimal. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h made the H dinner as a thank you, and when she knocked on his door an OW answered. The H said that the OW showed up unexpectedly and uninvited, but she did create some mild drama for the h and H.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Drug use by side character, child neglect, alcoholism by side character, and kidnapping. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had good closure with a cute jump ahead epilogue and a HEA.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I started out listening to the audiobook that was included with my scribed subscription, but ended up paying the $5.99 for the ebook on Amazon.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> I'd say that this is <u>Safe</u> for most readers.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the h pushing the H away<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_263778086" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/263778086?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=books-kelly-and-baba-liked-or-loved">books-kelly-and-baba-liked-or-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=hottest-alpha-males-ever">hottest-alpha-males-ever</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer263778086" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16401069777839357607"><b>UPDATE: Rating edited September 21, 2013. From 5 stars downgraded to 4 stars.</b><br/><br/>****************************************************<br/><br/>Mitch said to Billy<br/><b>"What I mean is, I didn't fall in love with you all as a whole. I fell in love with each of you because of who you are. I don't care about you because you come with Mara. I care about you because you're a good kid. You're smart. You're loyal. And you love and look out for your sister and Mara. I know grown men who do not have a character as fine as y</b></span>
  <span id="freeText16401069777839357607" style="display:none"><b>UPDATE: Rating edited September 21, 2013. From 5 stars downgraded to 4 stars.</b><br /><br />****************************************************<br /><br />Mitch said to Billy<br /><b>"What I mean is, I didn't fall in love with you all as a whole. I fell in love with each of you because of who you are. I don't care about you because you come with Mara. I care about you because you're a good kid. You're smart. You're loyal. And you love and look out for your sister and Mara. I know grown men who do not have a character as fine as yours. Those are the reasons I love you. There are different reasons I love Billie. And there are different reasons I love Mara. Today, what we had together was good. But the feelings I feel for you aren't feelings I have to have in order to have Mara. They're feelings you earned. Now, you with me?" <br /><br />Oh, yes, I'm with you, Mitch! Always.</b><br /><br />Seriously, I need a bigger heart. I promised so many KA heroes a little part of my heart and it's getting tight in there. Anyway, what can I say? Super gorgeous, super hot, and super <b>gentle</b> Mitch Lawson is my <i>DREAM DAD!</i> Wow, I loved Law Man! It's another wonderful story written by the absolutely amazing Kristen Ashley! <br /><br /><i>Brief synopsis</i><br />Mara Hanover is a salesperson and is working for Pierson's Mattress and Bed (oh, yeah, my dirty mind is wandering again). Mara has a secret crush on <i>Ten Point Five</i> Detective Mitch Lawson since he moved across her breezeway four years ago. BTW, Mara's got a <i>One to Ten Classification System.</i> One day Mara's faucet won't turn off and unfortunately she is totally clueless (among other things) when it comes to plumbing. Nice guy Mitch offers to help her.<br /><br />Mara's cousin Bill has two kids. Billy (the boy) and Billie (the girl). Bill is a bad Dad and occasionally Billy and Billie are running away and are calling Mara to help them out. When Mara needs to get them away from her cousin's mess, Detective Mitch Lawson is ready to do anything to help her and the kids. Mara is pretty stunned and insecure. She thinks that <i>Ten Point Fives</i> don't help out <i>Two Point Fives.</i> That was law in <i>Mara World.</i><br /><br />*******************<br />Mara could be a bit annoying at times. Every time Mitch gave her a compliment, she freaked out and twisted it into something bad. Admittedly, I had to cut her some slack since her self-esteem was almost non-existent. Mara had a bad childhood and she thinks that <i>Ten Point Five</i> super hot, super gorgeous, super masculine Mitch is waaaay out of her league because she is only a <i>Two Point Five.</i> Of course gorgeous Mitch thinks differently and I'm absolutely sure that he wouldn't mind your "illegal" maneuver, Mara! <i>Okey dokey, clue the f*ck in, sweetheart, before you wake up and wonder where your life has gone!</i><br /><br />While I loved the first 60 % of the story, the last 40 % turned out to be simply fabulous! Mitch is ten kinds of awesome! There are so many, many memorable and heart-warming moments. Mitch may have soulful eyes but I think this guy is simply soulful as all get out! Yes, he is very alpha, yet Mitch is such a good and incredibly gentle guy. Right to his very core. I love, love this man! I've read many KA books and I have to say that Mitch is probably the gentlest of all her heroes. He is different and he said the sweetest things. It was a very nice surprise. Mitch was the perfect match for the somewhat shy yet wonderful Mara! About 68 % into the story there is an AMAZING heart-to-heart between these two! Then again, I think the best aspect of Law Man was the interaction between Mitch and the kids. I even added a new shelf and it's labeled "dream-dad". Mitch, you have my utmost respect! He proved himself worthy of being a "father". I really could feel the patience and love, and Mitch never ever hesitated to show his deepest emotions and feelings! So beautiful! As always Kristen writes wonderful main and secondary characters. I loved the build-up. It's well done and their chemistry was superb! On top of that, you will enjoy many witty, hilarious, and thoughtful dialogs. Here's an advice to those who weep easily. Just keep some tissues handy!<br /><br />Here are a few memorable moments, and believe me there were so many, many more!<br /><br /><i>"I'll go gentle, baby," he whispered against my lips. "I promise. You'll always be safe with me."<br />Oh. My.<br />"Mitch," I breathed.<br />His soulful eyes held mine captive as he repeated firmly, "Always."<br /><br />"Let's see if I can tear that cocoon wide open and let my Mara fly."<br /><br />"You're Mara, you're sweet, you're beautiful and I will not forget until the day I die how beautiful it felt to slide inside you with you wrapped around me, see your eyes get wet and know straight in my gut that you felt how beautiful it was too."<br /><br />"Best thing that ever happened to me, that shredded washer," he whispered.<br />"Too bad I didn't know what a washer was or I would have shredded it myself," I whispered back and he burst out laughing.</i><br /><br />Mitch made many of my womanly parts tingle. If you want to feel it too then I can only give you one advice. Read it!!!<br /><br />On a personal note:<br />Kane "Tack" Allen made an appearance together with Cabe "Hawk" Delgado in Law Man. Kane said to Mara: <i>"Wonderin' how I keep missin' my shot at the good ones."</i> Kane, I am so glad that you'll find your special woman in Motorcycle Man! I'm in love with this guy since Mystery Man and I can't wait to read his story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16401069777839357607" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
