        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3545501062" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13893169304804373500">Okay ,wow how did I write a review for this book months ago, but left it in my drafts without posting it... <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522144106ra/25280010.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>– <b>
  <i>4.5 stars</i>
</b><br/><br/>↬ <b>
  <u>MITCHELL JAMES LAWSON</u>
</b> (H)<br/> <br/>Mitch is <b>MY</b> man! <br/> <br/><b>P</b>: the perfect man doesn't exist<br/><b>Kristen Ashley</b>: wait hold my beer <br/> <br/>Honestly I don't know what to say except that I feel like i'm cheating on Lahn with Mitchell.  Mitchell must be in my TOP 5 fav heroes of 2020. He is no Law Man, he is THE Man. 😭 <br/> <br/>Mitch is the detective living in the same apartment complex as Mara and he had h</span>
  <span id="freeText13893169304804373500" style="display:none">Okay ,wow how did I write a review for this book months ago, but left it in my drafts without posting it... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522144106ra/25280010.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>– <b>
  <i>4.5 stars</i>
</b><br><br>↬ <b>
  <u>MITCHELL JAMES LAWSON</u>
</b> (H)<br> <br>Mitch is <b>MY</b> man! <br> <br><b>P</b>: the perfect man doesn't exist<br><b>Kristen Ashley</b>: wait hold my beer <br> <br>Honestly I don't know what to say except that I feel like i'm cheating on Lahn with Mitchell.  Mitchell must be in my TOP 5 fav heroes of 2020. He is no Law Man, he is THE Man. 😭 <br> <br>Mitch is the detective living in the same apartment complex as Mara and he had his eyes set on her for years. After an incident with a broken washer, Mitch is finally making a move and boy was it smooth. Mitch knew exactly what to say to get Mara out of her shell. Mitch knew her so well from years of watching her, he already knew that she has a crush on him but is too shy. <br> <br>Every time Mara was trying to get out of spending time with Mitch, he was like <i>"Naaah sorry baby, I can't hear you and I don't want to hear you, because the things that are stuck in your head are too whacked for your own good. I'm just going to force you to spend time with me whether you like it or not"</i>. It was comical how Mitch literally gave zero fucks what Mara wanted and not in a way that he doesn't care about her wants, but it was the only way to get her out of her own world. <br> <br>When Mitch saw that Mara has problems with her cousin Bill and his two children, Mitch took charge without blinking an eye to help her with taking care of them. They both literally jumped into parenthood without any experience while not even be together. Mara doesn't even have a choice, cause she's the one who always took care about Billy and Billie when their father fucked up, but Mitch has a choice to walk away. Mitch and Mara are not even a couple yet, but Mitch took care of all of them without complain. <u>I LOVE HIM!</u> <br> <br>His relationship with Billie: 🥺💕🥺💕🥺💕🥺<br>His relationship with Billy: 🥺💕🥺💕🥺💕🥺<br>Mitch and Mara acting like an old married couple: 🥺💕🥺💕🥺💕🥺💕🥺💕🥺💕🥺<br><blockquote>
  <b>“That's another thing that doesn't turn me off, sweetheart, knowin' that you come with those kids and you need to know that. You also need to know I want kids of my own, two of them. But I don't care, if this works out between me and you, that the kids we have will have an older brother and sister that don't have my blood, just my heart.”</b>
</blockquote> <br> <br>Just give that man a medal on being the best. Bye. <br><br>This book is called Law Man, because Mitch is a detective, but I was wondering if the Law in Lawson is a coincidence or not. 🤔<br> <br>↬ <b>
  <u>MARABELLE JOLENE HANOVER</u>
</b> (h)<br> <br>I wanted to smack this girl <u>SO</u> hard. <br> <br>Mara got this whacked idea in her head where she categorized each person into a 1 to 10 scale depending on their attractivness and personality. And only the same categories can get involed with each other. That means if you're a 10, you can only be together with 9s or 10s or sometimes even a 8 but that's already slumming and will not last longterm. <br>  <br>For some reasons, her background is an important factor here, Mara thinks she is a two, maybe a three, so she's a Two Point Five. Mitchell in her eyes is a Ten, maybe Eleven that means a Ten Point Five and people like him don't hang out with people like her. <br> <br>Every time she thinks about herself as a Two Point Five, I wanted to smack her. That means in total I wanted to smack her 27 times. I wanted to reach into the book and shake Mara so badly and scream: <i>"SHUT THE FUCK UP!!!</i> You're not in a Black Mirror episode where it is 2089. The society doesn't categorize you into different categories where you're only allowed to hang out with people that have the same level as you. This is not some game where you get point when you do something good or where points get deducted when you do something bad. PEOPLE CHANGE BISSsshhHhH you don't get stuck on some level your whole life. Jeez, girl get your head outta your ass!"<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1518726865ra/25067279.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Mara's mother used to belittle her and look down on her daughter and maaaybe there is some truth in the saying 'if you hear something often enough, you start to believe it' buut damn how annoying it was even if I can understand why she is the way she is. For that reason I try not to read about shy heroines, because their self-esteem is usually rock bottom and I can't deal with this shit. Every girl should think of herself as a Queen. Period. Period. PERIODTTT. <br> <br>A big reason why I'm giving this book only 4 stars despite really loving it, is because Mara was such a pain in the ass. Now I can say I love her, but maaan it took a while until I could fully embrace her. <br>BUUUT when Mara finally got to the point when she saw her worth and telling her haters off. It was a sight to behold. There is that one scene where she stood up for herself and I was screaming at my kindle, cause I was so proud of her *wipe tears off my eyes* That's my girl. <br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>And I did this mostly because if he told me to throw myself in front of a train, but did it adding the word "baby", I would have done it.</b>
</blockquote><br>--&gt; same girl same. I hate the endearment "baby" but out of Mitch mouth idc. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1603841069ra/30297807.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>↬ <b>
  <u>THE FAMILY DYNAMIC</u>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I love you, Bud," he whispered to Billy and two more tears escaped.<br>"I love you too, Mitch," Billy whispered back, my breath hitched and both males' eyes came to me.<br>I waved my wineglass at them and murmured, "Don't mind me. Have your moment."<br>Mitch leaned back, letting Billy go and grinning at me. "Men don't have moments."<br>"You do," I returned. "I'm witnessing one."<br>"This isn't a moment, honey, it's a meeting of the minds," Mitch contradicted me.”</b>
</blockquote><br>I'm doing it backward and give some background info about the plot now. Basically the whole plot of this book is that Mara is getting guardianship of her two cousins Billy (boy) and Billie (girl) after running away for the x-times from their father. You can imagine what kind of father Bill is who named their children Billy and Billerina. Mara and Mitch take Billy and Billie away from their home and move them into Mara's home. Law Man doesn't have any OM/OW drama, but a lot of drama revolving around the children and how Bill and other people are making Mara's life harder than it should be. <br> <br>This book is pretty much all about Mara, Mitch, Billy and Billie being domestic for 500+ pages and it was *sparkles* WHOLESOME *sparkles. There are so many scenes of them having dinner together, going on trips, playing baseball etc. and it's the best thing I've read in a long time. I LOVE KIDS in books, especially kids like Billie and Billy. Half of the time I wanted Mitch and Mara to adopt ME and the other half I wanted to adopt the kids MYSELF. <br> <br>Billie is just a ball of energy and literally happy about EVERYTHING. It doesn't take much to make her happy. She's a ray of sunshine. I love her so much. Billy is as much adorable. He is more of a quiet and observant soul. He is 11 going on 111 with how old his soul really is. Every time Billy was on screen I'm like *insert a lot of pleading emojis*. So far he had to take care of his lil sister and now that he is with Mara, Billy wants to be the best kid possible and there are not enough words to describe how much I love this boy who thinks he has to carry all responsibility on his back *insert cry emoji* <br> <br>Mitch and Mara's relationship with the kids *chef's kiss* + Mitch and Mara acting like an old married couple from the beginning = HAPPY PHUONG <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437452315ra/15586741.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Kristen Ashley's writing is so minimalistic. It's not poetic or anything. With how long her books are, her writing gets repetitive a lot. The romance is also very insta-lovey most of the time,  a trope I'm not very fond of, but damn the way I always feel so happy whenever I pick up any of KA's books that I couldn't give a shit about any of these flaws. I'm OBSESSED with KA Heroes. They are all so swoony and protective and have my unyielding love and devotion. <br><blockquote>
  <b>“What I mean is, I didn't fall in love with you all as a whole. I fell in love with each of you because of who you are. I don't care about you because you come with Mara. I care about you because you're a good kid. You're smart. You're loyal. And you love and look out for your sister and Mara. I know grown men who do not have a character as fine as yours. Those are the reasons I love you. There are different reasons I love Billie. And there are different reasons I love Mara. Today, what we had together was good. But the feelings I feel for you aren't feelings I have to have in order to have Mara. They're feelings you earned. Now, you with me?”</b>
</blockquote><br>i- 🥺🥺🥺🥺 <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1603841793ra/30297841.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>P.S.: Why do these covers look like KA locked her children in a room with only Microsoft Paint, told them to have fun and experiment a little?<br> <br>P.P.S.: The day I stop making these comments about ugly ass covers is the day you know this account is getting hacked. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13893169304804373500" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_649577481" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/649577481" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/649577481?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Kristen Ashley Fans, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer649577481" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10145391171642774773"><b> 4 What Mitch Sees Makes It Worth It Stars<br/>* * * * <i> Spoiler Free<br/>QUICK BEFORE IT'S GONE, ONLY $2.99!!!</i><br/>This was a re-read for me and it was interesting to see my reactions were from the first time. I was in a book slump and trying to figure out what to read... and decided to visit a few books that I knew would be like slipping on a warm, comfy top that would surround me with warmth.<br/><br/>Kristen Ashley, for me never disappoints...let me rephrase... She has books which will always be a solid 5 and that wi</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10145391171642774773" style="display:none"><b> 4 What Mitch Sees Makes It Worth It Stars<br>* * * * <i> Spoiler Free<br>QUICK BEFORE IT'S GONE, ONLY $2.99!!!</i><br>This was a re-read for me and it was interesting to see my reactions were from the first time. I was in a book slump and trying to figure out what to read... and decided to visit a few books that I knew would be like slipping on a warm, comfy top that would surround me with warmth.<br><br>Kristen Ashley, for me never disappoints...let me rephrase... She has books which will always be a solid 5 and that will never change... she also has books which sometimes feel a little less...<br><br>But all of her books have moments- grand statements about life, love and knowing a certain rightness. Law Man had them and it made the story worthwhile.<br><br>Also, she is the Queen of Epilogues.<br><br>A nod to Mitch...</b>who at first was more Cave Man than remembered but was the true hero in this tale. His patience with Mara was close to saintly. The main thing was her devotion to cousins, Billy and Billie, with a passion that was tangible. Her "Mara World" was understandable coming from where she came... and she had the determination to get away from all of it. <br><br>I was up and down about how I felt with this as the way it was written was almost like reading a screenplay instead of a book. Meaning, every action, feeling and thought was described. It is the way of Ashley's writing but in this book... it felt a bit overdone causing me to lower my rating to 4 instead of 5 from a couple of years ago. <br> <br>So I am now re-reading all of the Dream Men and because it is my quirky way- not in order...<br>I am off to read Wild Man and then maybe Mystery Man and then the one I so enjoy, Motorcycle Man. <br>I don't know if I will do full reviews... only will if I think I have something to add to all the other reviews out there.<br>Brock, hold on... I am on my way to ya. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1483487036l/12299419._SX50_.jpg" alt="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1409039191" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1622243865588061688"><b>2.5 **<u>um and ah</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444077615i/16448854.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ok, we all know I'm a big KA fan, but that was a study in patience. I can't even explain how I managed to get through some of the major parts of this book. It started difficult to stomach and didn't get much better along the way. Although I have to say, the last 20% were right up my alley and seeing all of our old friends made me a little giddy, it didn't help the story as a whole. I'm sorry to say this might just be my least favourite KA book. <br/><br/>The heroine was unbearable. </span>
  <span id="freeText1622243865588061688" style="display:none"><b>2.5 **<u>um and ah</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444077615i/16448854.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok, we all know I'm a big KA fan, but that was a study in patience. I can't even explain how I managed to get through some of the major parts of this book. It started difficult to stomach and didn't get much better along the way. Although I have to say, the last 20% were right up my alley and seeing all of our old friends made me a little giddy, it didn't help the story as a whole. I'm sorry to say this might just be my least favourite KA book. <br><br>The heroine was unbearable. Mara has low self-esteem, lives in her own little world, with her own little rating system and is in love with her neighbour Mitch Lawson. The latter being one of her more appealing traits. I have to say, being in her head all the time was not a nice thing. She was introduced as one of those struck stupid by hot guy girls. One look at Mitch and she was speechless and lost braincells by the minute. Of course that let up after a while, but her insecurities were almost too much to bear.<br><br>I guess in hindsight, listening to the audiobook was a good idea and the only thing that kept me on track and actually made me finish the book. Of course Mitch was a yummy alpha male just like Ms. Ashley always writes them, but that alone doesn’t make a good read. Next to Mitch I have to point out Billy and Billie. The cutest little things. But oh god Mara...if only Mara was someone else entirely. Shame, such a shame.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1779315045" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1779315045" />
    <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog"><img alt="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420222674p2/38657470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1779315045?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog">Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18888391-law-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=4-and-a-half-stars">4-and-a-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=audio-books">audio-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1779315045" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1390363153444601332"><b>4.5 stars! Audio book</b><br/><br/>I’m a total rebel. I’m reading this series out of order. Shhh. <br/><br/>Here’s what I’ve discovered about Kristen Ashley books based on the limited number I’ve read. Kristen writes long-ass books. She takes her time weaving intricate stories, establishing the complexities of unique characters, and delving into ever evolving relationships. That can make for some stellar reading, but a 500 page book requires a lot of dedication. In the case of Law Man, the payoff is worth it.<br/><br/>I’m not on</span>
  <span id="freeText1390363153444601332" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars! Audio book</b><br><br>I’m a total rebel. I’m reading this series out of order. Shhh. <br><br>Here’s what I’ve discovered about Kristen Ashley books based on the limited number I’ve read. Kristen writes long-ass books. She takes her time weaving intricate stories, establishing the complexities of unique characters, and delving into ever evolving relationships. That can make for some stellar reading, but a 500 page book requires a lot of dedication. In the case of Law Man, the payoff is worth it.<br><br>I’m not one of those people who swoons over alpha a-holes, and I know Kristen Ashley can gravitate towards them. You know the type. They’re super hot, but they’re domineering, arrogant, rude, and sometimes downright mean—at least in the beginning. Mitch is tenacious and demanding, but there’s an innate kindness about him. Mara’s life is a hot mess, and whether she’s willing to admit it or not, she needs someone with a firm yet loving hand to take charge.<br><br>Mara’s extreme shyness and her stubbornness can be irritating at times. There are definitely moments she tested my patience. However, her insecurities are so ingrained, justified, and understandable that I found her to be endearing overall. <br><br>The plot plays out in a lengthy fashion, but I was never bored. I’m allergic to insta-love, so I think the simmering nature of the romance is all the more enjoyable for its sense of realism. <br><br>The variety of colorful characters is absolute perfection. Billy and Billie? Forget about it! I was over the moon for those kids. Mitch and Mara’s friends are wonderful and bring lots of additional humor to this sweet story. If you’re looking for heartwarming moments, you’ll hit the jackpot with the epilogue.<br><br>I chose to go with the audio book version, and I think that was a smart choice. Narration is an art form and when it’s well done, it feels like aural theatre. Kate Russell is a phenomenal voice actor. Her narration conveys the heart of each character, making them come alive in very distinct ways.<br><br>Well done, all the way around!<br><br><a href="http://readingfrenzyblog.com" target="”_blank”" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458784026i/18530130.jpg" alt="Reading Frenzy Book Blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1390363153444601332" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_334943124" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/334943124" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/334943124?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer334943124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer207269998373704197">4.5 stars<br/><br/><b> <i> “Mara, I’m keepin’ you safe. I’m keepin’ those kids safe and you don’t have a choice in that, sweetheart. Thats just the way it’s gonna be… I was made to protect you and you were made in the way that it would always be worth it.” </i></b>  ~Mitch<br/><br/>Oh *swoon*, Mitch has stolen my heart!! Seriously hot, family oriented, loving, swoony, drool-worhty badass Alpha cop <br/><br/>I’ll be honest, the first 70% of the book was a 4 star read for me, but the last 30% was fully 5 stars!<br/><br/>Mara and Mitch live in the sam</span>
  <span id="freeText207269998373704197" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br><br><b> <i> “Mara, I’m keepin’ you safe. I’m keepin’ those kids safe and you don’t have a choice in that, sweetheart. Thats just the way it’s gonna be… I was made to protect you and you were made in the way that it would always be worth it.” </i></b>  ~Mitch<br><br>Oh *swoon*, Mitch has stolen my heart!! Seriously hot, family oriented, loving, swoony, drool-worhty badass Alpha cop <br><br>I’ll be honest, the first 70% of the book was a 4 star read for me, but the last 30% was fully 5 stars!<br><br>Mara and Mitch live in the same apartment complex. They have each been crushing on each other secretly for the past 4 years but for various reasons have never acted on them. When, one day, Mara suddenly gets a desperate call from her dead beat cousin’s two little children, Billie (girl) and Billy (boy), saying that they ran away from their home and need her help, she runs off to rescue them and Mitch comes with her. Mara suddenly ends up with custody of them and Mitch is willing to do everything in his power to help her and the kids. Serious drama ensues involving the Russian mob, druggie trailer trash, custody battles, family issues, as well as a swoon-worthy romance, a whole lot of healing, and the heart-warming building of a beautiful, if unconventional, family unit held together by whole lotta love and earned trust.<br><br><i> “I’ll go gentle, baby,” he whispered against my lips. “I promise. You’ll always be safe with me.<br>Oh. My. <br>“Mitch,” I breathed.<br>His soulful eyes held mine captive as he repeated firmly, “Always.” </i><br><br>The only thing in this book that dragged that first 70% down for me was Mara. Although I loved her, and she was very sweet and caring, she really got on my nerves with her insistence on always finding reasons why things shouldn’t work out with Mitch and for her serious self-esteem issues. But once she came around, things took a drastic turn up.<br><br>I absolutely ADORED seeing how whole heartedly Mitch adopted the kids into his life. His commitment and love for them and Mara gave me chills and shivers and the conviction with which he went about convincing Mara that he wanted this was beautiful and totally adorable!!<br><br><i> “That's another thing that doesn't turn me off, sweetheart, knowin' that you come with those kids and you need to know that. You also need to know I want kids of my own, two of them. But I don't care, if this works out between me and you, that the kids we have will have an older brother and sister that don't have my blood, just my heart.” </i><br><br>And I loved the effort he went to to help heal the kids of the scars of their previous home and to comfort them with the concrete knowledge that with him and Mara, they were loved, cared for and wanted.<br><br><i> “The man who gets Mara gets you and Billie. I’m that man. What you gotta get is, while fallin’ in love with Mara, I fell in love with you and your sister. Straight up, Bud, no lie. The feelings I feel for Mara are hers, the feelings I feel for Billie are hers and the feelings I feel for you are yours. You all have my love, not collectively, individually. Do you understand me?” </i><br><br>And as with the previous books of the series, we get to see all the characters we have come to adore from this world working together and honestly, it was Totally. Badass. Swoon. Overload that left me clutching at my heart!!!! Hawk and Gwen had a seriously hot and swoony cameo, and we get to see Brock and Tess as well. And when the big drama goes down at the end, Tack and his badass biker boys step in and boy did his scenes make me just dying to read his book!!!!<br><br>And WOW!! That epilogue!!!!!! I had the hugest grin on my face for the whole of it and then at the very last line of the book, the happy tears just started rolling!<br><br>Here's how I see Mitch and Mara:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378597i/734290._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my review, come visit <a href="http://http//aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>Or come take a peek at <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">my blog's Facebook page </a></span>
  <a data-text-id="207269998373704197" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1617007029?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18888391-law-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2020">2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=audible-owned">audible-owned</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1617007029" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8495472889781593373">This is by far my favorite in this series. Mitch Lawson is one of the best heroes I've read. The way he handled Mara and the way he didn't hesitate at all to jump right in and help her take care of her two little cousins was amazing. I'm such a sucker for a guy with kids, especially when they are so good with them and how protective Mitch was.<br/><br/>I really liked Mara as well. While she did have some major insecurity issues, she is also valid to have them with the way she was treated as a child. I get</span>
  <span id="freeText8495472889781593373" style="display:none">This is by far my favorite in this series. Mitch Lawson is one of the best heroes I've read. The way he handled Mara and the way he didn't hesitate at all to jump right in and help her take care of her two little cousins was amazing. I'm such a sucker for a guy with kids, especially when they are so good with them and how protective Mitch was.<br /><br />I really liked Mara as well. While she did have some major insecurity issues, she is also valid to have them with the way she was treated as a child. I get why her insecurities would be annoying but I find that if the reason is valid, I don't take issue with it. Add to that, Mitch handled her insecurities in a way that I loved.<br /><br />Billy and Billie are another reason why I loved this book so much. I love when there are kids in a book if it's done right and KA did it right. I loved their little personalities. They brought a lot to this story and really enhanced why I loved the main couple so much. I was actually sad that I finished the book. I wanted more.<br /><br />I did a re-read with the audiobook and the narrator Kate Russell is a new favorite! She did such a good job with the kids voices. I think she enhanced this story.</span>

<div id="review_289891408" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/289891408" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/289891408?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Contemporary romance fans</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Auntee by: </span>
      Shawna
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=husband-worthy_hero">husband-worthy_hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2012_reads">2012_reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer289891408" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16899718191636278148">I almost gave up on this one. <i>Almost</i>...But with the encouragement of GR buddies/Kristen Ashley fans, I soldiered on, waiting (not so patiently) for the heroine, Mara, to (in Mitch's words) "get her head out of her ass". And I'm so glad I stuck with it, because by about the 60% mark, this book became un-put-down-able!<br/><br/>No big review here, just some thoughts/likes/dislikes...<br/><br/>The book started off well. I mean, who doesn't like a heroine who's a little unsure of herself, only to realize her worth when</span>
  <span id="freeText16899718191636278148" style="display:none">I almost gave up on this one. <i>Almost</i>...But with the encouragement of GR buddies/Kristen Ashley fans, I soldiered on, waiting (not so patiently) for the heroine, Mara, to (in Mitch's words) "get her head out of her ass". And I'm so glad I stuck with it, because by about the 60% mark, this book became un-put-down-able!<br><br>No big review here, just some thoughts/likes/dislikes...<br><br>The book started off well. I mean, who doesn't like a heroine who's a little unsure of herself, only to realize her worth when the man of her dreams shows interest in her? But Mara...oh boy...she just really annoyed me. I knew when she described herself as a "2.5" repeatedly, that I was going to have trouble with her. This girl had the <i>lowest</i> self-esteem/opinion of herself of any character that I've ever read. And I knew there had to be a reason (and believe me, there was--she had a crappy childhood with the mother of all mothers), but I think KA waited just a little too long to reveal that reason. I mean, I was seriously getting <i>annoyed</i> with Mara, and her whole rating scale! And no amount of interest paid to her by the luscious Mitch, no amount of her friends, coworkers, boss, adoring young cousins expressing how wonderful she was would budge this stubborn woman into realizing her worth. Ack!<br><br>Thank God for Detective Mitch Lawson and his <i>patience</i> with Mara. I can't say enough about him...except to say he deserves a special place on my husband-worthy shelf. He's everything you want in a romance hero--sexy, understanding, patient, kind, good with kids, fabulous in bed, protective...who cares if sometimes he's a little bossy and dominant? I loved how he "got" Mara, I loved how he finally broke her out of her "cocoon", I loved how he was with her two young cousins (Billy and Billie)...I just loved everything about him. He was the reason I kept reading when Mara was working my last nerve.<br><br><i>I liked how Mitch taught Billy how to play ball...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=MarkRicketson6-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371685i/724801._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I also enjoyed meeting some characters from KA's other books. Since I've been reading her books out of order, I haven't met some of them yet. But oh boy, after reading Mara's description and reaction to Hawk...<i>I've got to read his book!</i> <b>Next</b>!<br><br>And oh yes, the epilogue. No spoilers here, except that it takes place <b>13 years later</b>...and...*big sigh*.<br><br>So my advice? Stick with this one. If Mara starts to irk you, just know that it gets better, she finally realizes her worth and how proud she should be with the life she made for herself. You're going to adore Mitch, and want a Mitch for yourself (that's a given). And you're going to love their HEA. 4 stars<br><br>P.S.: After reading this book, I really want to get a new mattress...:)</span>
  <a data-text-id="16899718191636278148" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2011994625" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2605344998126200676"><b>DNF @ 20%</b><br/> <br/><b>
  <i>*0.75 star because I can round up ratings too just like Mara*</i>
</b><br/> <br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446645809ra/16854510.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>*sigh*<br/> <br/>This is on me because I clearly had no business attempting to read this after my experience with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_' title='The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Gamble</a>. The number of times I’ve given ‘no no’ authors a second chance only for it to blow up in my face is just laughable.<br/> <br/>Why do I keep doing this? 😩<br/> <br/>Pretty much all the same gripes I had in The Gamble happened here. I could go on and on about the absurd writing flaws. The typos, poor grammar, bad punctuation, </span>
  <span id="freeText2605344998126200676" style="display:none"><b>DNF @ 20%</b><br> <br><b>
  <i>*0.75 star because I can round up ratings too just like Mara*</i>
</b><br> <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446645809ra/16854510.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>*sigh*<br> <br>This is on me because I clearly had no business attempting to read this after my experience with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227041.The_Gamble__Colorado_Mountain___1_" title="The Gamble (Colorado Mountain, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gamble</a>. The number of times I’ve given ‘no no’ authors a second chance only for it to blow up in my face is just laughable.<br> <br>Why do I keep doing this? 😩<br> <br>Pretty much all the same gripes I had in The Gamble happened here. I could go on and on about the absurd writing flaws. The typos, poor grammar, bad punctuation, run-ons, and all the ‘uming’ ‘uhing’ the heroine keeps stuttering out. But I won’t. Just read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1008717376?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">my Gamble review</a>. <br><br>Same issue I had with the last one I had here, the heroine Mara acted like a confused child where everything needed to be explained to her by the hero. <i>
  <b>Literally</b>
</i> explained. And the hero walks all over her and talks to her like she's a simpleton, which I honestly couldn't blame in this case. I just don’t understand what KA was attempting to show by this? Are her heroines only gifted with their brains once they meet the hero? How charming. 😒 The fact that a grown woman couldn’t comprehend why her druggie adult cousin was arrested because he had drug paraphernalia out and with kids around just boggles my mind. Seriously Mara??? Jesus. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527281520ra/25597463.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>The problem with KA’s storytelling is that the first person narration sounds like it’s coming from an overeager toddler who is telling you about their day in rambling, incoherent, verbal diarrhea pointless detail and getting hung up on the smallest things that has no relevance to the overall story. And repeating themselves. CONSTANTLY. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497583172ra/23040265.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> It takes a whole paragraph to say one thing that can be said in <b>one.👏 single.👏 sentence</b>.👏 <br><i>How</i> is this author so popular? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503074264ra/23626566.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Get an editor Kristen Ashley, please! Because I promise you, nobody needs to know exactly how the heroine positions her body or places her elbows when she's fucking standing and talking. 😒 I get the overall picture just fine. <br><br>In this case:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497497134ra/23028683.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Now why I gave this a chance? Because of the blurb. I’m such a helpless sucker for shy awkward heroines and the whole neighbor thing was another element I usually enjoy. But this rubbed me the wrong way right off the bat and I’ll tell you why. The heroine Mara.<br> <br>For someone who is supposedly very shy and very insecure about themselves, please explain to me why this girl is going around rating people based on their looks?? I would love for KA to explain it because this just seriously blew my mind.<br><i>
  <blockquote>
<br>Roberta had been a Seven when I met her because she was pretty, petite, with thick brunette hair and a little extra weight that she held well. She was also happy with her family and her husband in their suburban house with two cars and vacations to Disney World. She'd slipped down to a Five Point Five when she got angry and moody and hated the world and mostly all the men in it after her husband left. Now she was back up and surpassed the Seven to be an Eight because she'd settled into her new life...</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497503988ra/23028934.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <blockquote>I didn't understand what she was saying, but explaining to her what the likes of me meant was was explaining to her my One to Ten Classification System. I didn't want to do that, especially explaining where I felt I came in on the scale.<br>I'd learned not to share this information, because friends who cared about you always tried to talk you into believing you were so far up that scale it was unreal. My oldest friend, Lynette, who still lived back in Iowa, was the only person I'd told about my system. She even tried to talk me into believing I topped the scale at Mitch's rank of Ten Point Five. She was convinced of it and tried to convince me. I knew she was wrong and I knew she was convinced I was a Ten Point Five because she liked me. I liked her too. She was a definite Eight Point Five. When she was in a good mood and her sunny disposition shone even more brightly, she soared up to a Nine Point Five, she had nothing to worry about.</blockquote>
</i><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497504865ra/23028961.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now just imagine this kind of observation on the very first page of the book. I literally thought it was the hero's POV with the side-eyeing and internal rating system and had to re-read it a couple of times to understand. But no, this was all coming from 'sweet shy' skittery as a deer Mara. Apparently someone who is so messed up in their head about their own looks and how others view her, she thinks it's totally fine to go around giving mental scores on others appearances.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407507561ra/10731407.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Excuse my bluntness but I just found this character so fucking <b>stupid</b>. <br><br>And a total <b>useless asshole</b>.<br><br>She's an insult to shy, insecure, awkward women in real life. The lack of intelligence she displayed in just the first 50 pages is astoundingly painful.<br><i>
  <blockquote>"Mitch, the kids-" I breathed.<br>"First, we're goin' to Lola's and giving them a good meal."<br>I blinked at him.<br>Lola's?<br>Lola's?<br>Lola's was awesome and had absolutely fantastic food, but it was also not what the kids were used to. It wasn't fancy, but it wasn't Taco Bell, either, and it wasn't exactly inexpensive. I hadn't actually asked Mitch to accompany me, but since he did, I thought we'd pop to the nearest fast-food joint, go through a drive-thru and get the kids home. After, I would do whatever it was I was going to have to do at Bill's, then get home and away from Mitch.</blockquote>
</i>Right. Take the kids back to a housebroken home after feeding them the <u>same junk food</u> they always eat at home (if they are lucky). G-d forbid the idea of a good decent restaurant should have ever entered your skull without macho Mitch around. And hey asshole: How is dumping the kids back home with their neglectful father fixing the issue you just said you needed to step in and fix? 🙈<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497506486ra/23029010.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <blockquote>"You stood me up."<br>"I didn't."<br>"Mara, you did and you did it, essentially, twice."<br>My head jerked to face him again and I snapped, "No, I didn't!"<br>He shook his head and muttered, "Jesus, you got your head so far up your ass it's a wonder you can breathe."<br>"Pardon?" I hissed.<br>"You heard me."<br>"Yes," I bit out, "I did, and what you said was not very nice."<br>"No, baby, it wasn't but it was the fuckin' truth."<br>Was I sitting in Detective Mitch Lawson's SUV fighting with him? Two Point Fives didn't fight with Ten Point Fives. It was against the laws of the universe. How did this happen?<br>"I don't have my head up my ass!" I snapped somewhat loudly.<br>"You live in a whole different world," he retorted.<br>"Do not!"</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497506486ra/23029011.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <blockquote>"He's still got that guy comin' over all the time, and I don't like him. He's a creep. And I don't like him around Billie. He's sugar sweet to her and it freaks me out. Gives her candy. Tells her she's pretty. It's weird."<br>Billy had been telling me about "that guy" for a while, and Billy had good instincts, so I figured whoever "that guy" was, he wasn't a good guy. And what he said about how "that guy" treated Billie made my stomach clench and my mouth taste sour. </blockquote>
</i><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497558752ra/23037324.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Your nine-year old cousin has been telling you a creep has been hanging around his six year old sister for <i>months</i> and you haven't done shit about it since <b>now</b>? <br><i>
  <blockquote>He didn't hide his liquor from me or his kids, which was something I didn't like. I knew how weird and uncomfortable it was seeing a parent drink all the time, drink until they were fall-down, crazy, stupid and sometimes mean drunk. And I didn't want that for Billy and Billie. <b>But it wasn't illegal</b>, and to my knowledge it didn't happen often.</blockquote>
</i><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497582743ra/23040090.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I seriously started to question how this woman got out of bed everyday and dressed herself.<br><i>
  <blockquote>I moved, opened the door a bit and stood in it.<br>"Hey," I said, and the minute my eyes hit him, I again felt like crying.<br>They needed to separate the zones. Mandatory boundaries. Ones to Threes got Canada (because there were a lot of us and we needed the space). Fours to Sixes got the US. The fewer numbered Sevens to Tens got the sultry, tropical beauty of Mexico. If they separated us, things like this wouldn't happen and therefore hurt like this wouldn't be felt.</blockquote>
</i><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497737513ra/23054114.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <blockquote>"You need to quit talking," I blurted and wished I could clap my hands over my mouth because I sounded like a fool.<br>I should have lied to him earlier. I should have kicked him in the shin and run away.</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497737513ra/23054115.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <blockquote>"Mitch--"<br>He dumped the scrambled eggs into the waiting melted butter in the skillet and looked at me. "Get the butter and jelly baby."<br>I moved to the fridge and I did this mostly because if he told me to throw myself in front of a train but did it adding the word "baby," I would have done it.</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493877232ra/22661467.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mara Hanover is a complete waste of ink and paper IMO. <br> <br>So yeah. Lesson learned. <br><br>Me and Kristen Ashley books do not mix well. 👋👋👋👋<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460579145ra/18761839.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="2605344998126200676" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1583928484" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10373722517468890504"><strong>4.75 stars.</strong><br/><br/>It has been a while since I have read a Kristen Ashley book and I forgot how crazy good they are and also how much fun I have reading them.<br/>Mitch and Mara's story along with her distorted sense of self worth made for pretty interesting reading. All of her family growing up was trashy and verging on criminals and so even though she had left that life behind more than 13 years ago, her perception of herself hadn't changed with it.<br/>In her eyes Detective Mitch Lawson was a 10.5 and she was </span>
  <span id="freeText10373722517468890504" style="display:none"><strong>4.75 stars.</strong><br /><br />It has been a while since I have read a Kristen Ashley book and I forgot how crazy good they are and also how much fun I have reading them.<br />Mitch and Mara's story along with her distorted sense of self worth made for pretty interesting reading. All of her family growing up was trashy and verging on criminals and so even though she had left that life behind more than 13 years ago, her perception of herself hadn't changed with it.<br />In her eyes Detective Mitch Lawson was a 10.5 and she was a 2.5, therefore he couldn't be seriously interested in her ( I am assuming she was using a scale of 1-10, but it is KA so who the hell knows).<br />In "Mara's world" a mutual attraction between them just did not compute. <br />For some strange reason I seem to have read this series totally out of order. <br />This is the 3rd book but I started with book one and then book four and now only have book two left to read. <br /> This book was delightful and I think I found it so entertaining mainly because Mitch was such a super-sweet guy. For instance I really did like how it took a while for the relationship to develop between these two.<br />Mitch first had to work at breaking down all of Mara's barriers in order to get closer to her and his persistence in that respect was really satisfying to read about.<br />I also have to mention that this book has one of the sweetest epilogues ever IMO (totally loved it).</span>

<div id="review_859907977" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/859907977" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/859907977?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer859907977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17445644594439079666">On one hand you have very strong and sexy police detective Mitch Lawson, aka Mr. Ten Point Five, and on the other hand a very sweet but insecure salesperson Mara Hanover, aka Ms. Two Point Five. How can these two ever work things out so they can be together in the real world? <br/><br/>Well, it takes a jerky police detective to get them there. Now just stay with me...Mara is all kinds of sweet but she's had some things happen in her life that has messed her up and skewed her view of herself. There would n</span>
  <span id="freeText17445644594439079666" style="display:none">On one hand you have very strong and sexy police detective Mitch Lawson, aka Mr. Ten Point Five, and on the other hand a very sweet but insecure salesperson Mara Hanover, aka Ms. Two Point Five. How can these two ever work things out so they can be together in the real world? <br><br>Well, it takes a jerky police detective to get them there. Now just stay with me...Mara is all kinds of sweet but she's had some things happen in her life that has messed her up and skewed her view of herself. There would never ever be any Mitch and Mara if it was up to Mara...that's for sure. <br><br>You probably won't like Mitch for a bit. I certainly didn't. I couldn't imagine what everyone was going on about. <i>He's a big fat jerk</i>!! I really hate when men won't let women speak and he did a whole heck of a lot of that. Granted sometimes it was necessary but sometimes it would've been nice for them to just talk about things. But ~sigh~ that's the way of KA men. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393210776ra/8677100.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mara was a bit nuts! There's just no other way to describe her. She assigns points to people based on looks and they can go up and down depending on how they are. Also, people are in zones...1-3, 4-6, and 7-10 and the different zones cannot mix. This is called Mara World. She feels she's out of Mitch's league and there's no way he could possibly want anything out her and certainly not a relationship. <br><br>That would be all fine and dandy except some things happen and she becomes the guardian of her two cousins. Now everything is much different and this is where Mara won me over. She always puts the kids first...even if she doesn't know what to do or how she will do it. I do have to say that I was a bit taken back by how much Mitch wanted to be involved. <br><br>Yes, yes, yes....there are some steamy scenes. Mitch obviously knows what he's doing and him and Mara are great together. I got a big kick out of the LBD scene.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393211160ra/8677120.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There's some drama, of course, but for the most part, it's dealing with the kids and figuring out all that stuff along with starting a relationship. "Trailer Trash Twins" and "Roller Derby Rejects" was killing me! The last 15% things really hit the fan when we find out what Bill's dealings really involved. <br><br>Those were some real tear jerker moments for me...especially the scenes with Mitch and Bud. Wow...I just loved those. <br><br>There's some great secondary characters and naturally there's cross over characters from other books and series.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393211183ra/8677124.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And it wouldn't be a KA book without the wonderful epilogue. I was a bit surprised that it was thirteen years later though. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/610342.gif" width="250" height="020" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite Quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “Jesus fuckin’ <i>Christ</i>, baby, you can kiss.”<br> <br>♥ “Never believed in this shit but now, I’m thinkin’ I fell in love with the promise of you the first time I saw you.”<br><br>♥ “I love you, Bud," he whispered to Billy and two more tears escaped.<br><br>"I love you too, Mitch," Billy whispered back, my breath hitched and both males' eyes came to me.<br><br>I waved my wineglass at them and murmured, "Don't mind me. Have your moment."<br><br>Mitch leaned back, letting Billy go and grinning at me. "Men don't have moments."<br><br>"You do," I returned. "I'm witnessing one."<br><br>"This isn't a moment, honey, it's a meeting of the minds," Mitch contradicted me.” <br><br>♥ “Best thing that ever happened to me, that shredded washer,” he whispered. <br><br>“Too bad I didn’t know what a washer was or I would have shredded it myself,” I whispered back and he burst out laughing."</span>
  <a data-text-id="17445644594439079666" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review859907977">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/837076693?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacie" href="/user/show/15992420-stacie">Stacie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15992420-stacie?shelf=reread">reread</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer837076693" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6261414197559394067"><b>Reread Review December 19, 2018</b><br/><br/>I LOVE DETECTIVE MITCHELL JAMES LAWSON...still. 💓<br/><br/><b> Original Review June 11, 2014</b><br/><br/>OMG!! Detective Mitchell James Lawson! <br/>Ima try and keep this somewhat short because eeeeeekkkkkkk!!!, I'm finally about to get to Tack! <br/><br/>So... This is a really good book about something that happens way too often. And that is children needing someone to step in and take them out of a horrible situation, take care of them and love them unconditionally. Mara is very annoying at first but wh</span>
  <span id="freeText6261414197559394067" style="display:none"><b>Reread Review December 19, 2018</b><br /><br />I LOVE DETECTIVE MITCHELL JAMES LAWSON...still. 💓<br /><br /><b> Original Review June 11, 2014</b><br /><br />OMG!! Detective Mitchell James Lawson! <br />Ima try and keep this somewhat short because eeeeeekkkkkkk!!!, I'm finally about to get to Tack! <br /><br />So... This is a really good book about something that happens way too often. And that is children needing someone to step in and take them out of a horrible situation, take care of them and love them unconditionally. Mara is very annoying at first but when you find out where she is coming from she grows on you. Plus she stepped up with the kids and her self confidence grew by leaps and bounds. But what makes it so good is Detective Mitchell James Lawson. He is absolutely a dream man. Not just in a book dream man kind of way but a REAL LIFE Dream Man kind of way!! Meaning, if I didn't already have my very own real life dream man, I would be out looking for Detective Mitchell James Lawson right now! He is absolutely perfect, unflawed, and in no need of repair. He is not recovering from or in the middle of emotional or psychological trauma, he is not overly aggressive or controlling, though he does know when to take control, and he has a real life decent hard working important job where he makes a living for his family but is not rich. Real Life Dream Man. Absolutely going on the favorite males list. Now finally on to Tack who I already love, though probably not in a real life kind of way, but we shall see... Happy reading!!!<br /><br />PS. Just so you all know, I don't think there is anything wrong with a book only Dream Man. Sometimes the more messed up they are the better the book. Christian Grey anyone?...</span>
  <a data-text-id="6261414197559394067" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515675679" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13305566234323695265">4 For the Love of Mitch & Billy STARS!!!<br/>(BR w/Melissa, Denisse, Tiffany, and Elizabeth)<br/><br/><br/>Law Man is our hottie Detective Mitch Lawson's story.<br/>I was very much into Detective Lawson when we met him in "Mystery Man".<br/>He's been the secret obsession of his neighbor, Mara (Marabelle Jolene) Hanover for the past four years.<br/>They live across from each other in an apartment development.<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps40573ec3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396310413i/9115089._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps40573ec3.jpg' width='300' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Mara is a very shy, and VERY insecure woman!<br/>I swear that the reason I couldn't give this one a FIVE, was all because of </span>
  <span id="freeText13305566234323695265" style="display:none">4 For the Love of Mitch &amp; Billy STARS!!!<br>(BR w/Melissa, Denisse, Tiffany, and Elizabeth)<br><br><br>Law Man is our hottie Detective Mitch Lawson's story.<br>I was very much into Detective Lawson when we met him in "Mystery Man".<br>He's been the secret obsession of his neighbor, Mara (Marabelle Jolene) Hanover for the past four years.<br>They live across from each other in an apartment development.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps40573ec3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396310413i/9115089._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps40573ec3.jpg" width="300" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Mara is a very shy, and VERY insecure woman!<br>I swear that the reason I couldn't give this one a FIVE, was all because of how irritating and completely stupid she was.<br>She has a habit of rating everyone in her life and those around her.<br>Mitch is Mr Ten Point Five!<br>Mara sees herself as a Two Point Five and in Mara's World, Ten Point Fives and Two Point Fives don't mix.<br>They shouldn't even be breathing the same air.<br><br><br>The two finally interact after having been neighbors for the past four years when Mara's bathroom sink is leaking and Mitch comes over to take a look. <br>A family crisis occurs for Mara, and Mitch accompanies her to rescue her two little cousins.<br>Billie and Billy are her cousin Bill's young children and they often run away from home to get a hold of Mara, when their Dad has yet again neglected to feed them for days.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps09dab9ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396310413i/9115090._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps09dab9ec.jpg" width="350" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Mitch was completely swoon worthy to me in this story.<br>I loved how he swooped right in to protect Mara and the kids.<br>He had more patience than a Saint because Mara's stubbornness and stupidity really grated on my last nerve.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/860567_zps8c923864.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396310413ra/9115091.gif" alt=" photo 860567_zps8c923864.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I get she had a really horrible childhood and that her mother ingrained that low self esteem in her but many years had passed since she left her mother and old life behind.<br>EVERYONE could see just how beautiful she was and how much Mitch was into her...even the little kids!!!<br>She completely had her "Head Up Her Ass", as Mitch told her time and again.<br><br><br><br>The other thing that also was beyond annoying was Mara's inability to answer a simple question!<br>Everything was either an "UH" or "UM" from her!!<br><br><br>Mitch and little Billy made this book in my opinion!!<br>Mara eventually got her act together and I ended up liking her, but it took her almost the entire book to get there!!<br><br>Loved her interactions with Elvira, Gwen, Hawk, and Tack!!!<br><br>The epilogue was simply PERFECT!!<br>I'm so happy with how everyone ended up.<br>What a wonderful ending!!!<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I'll go gentle, baby,"</b>
</i> <b>he whispered against my lips.</b> <i>
  <b>"I promise. You will always be safe with me."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"Mara's World is fucked up and twisted, and my guess, that mother of yours and probably that aunt had somethin' to do with that. In the real world, the world everyone lives in, including you, honey, you and me make a whole fuckuva lot of sense."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><b>What met my eyes was the stuff posters were made of, but knowing the two beings filling my vision, I knew that what met my eyes were what dreams were made of.<br>How, on God's green earth, did my life shift so this vision could meet my eyes?</b> - Mara<br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"When you figure it out and move onto a beautiful life, don't regret the time you wasted on me."</b>
</i> - Mara<br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823406472" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13310360876869562901">There are those books that you re-read, but tend to skip through some parts. This is not one of those books for me. I read each chapter, each paragraph and each and every word. I love this book so much! Probably my favorite book, along with Rock Chick Regret, of all time and one of my most read.<br/><br/>***Re-read again.***<br/>I've been on a KA Dream Man series kick and have been re-reading these books. I have to say I LOVE my man Mitch! <br/>NOTE: Last re-read on 8/12/14</span>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3571498844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6081309886809162689">✰ <b>6++ stars</b> ✰<br/><br/>It’s ironic how, before I decided to pick up Law Man, I’ve been wanting to read KA books for some time but was intimidated because of the amount of books she has, not knowing where to start, but, now that I was able get a glimpse of her writing (<i>and absolutely loved it</i>), I’ve learned to appreciate that fact because it only means I have so much more books to look forward to - and it’s all thanks to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/41864935-melissa' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mel</a> for helping me where to start or I’d have been a lost cause lmaoo <33<br/><br/><b>I didn’t need</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6081309886809162689" style="display:none">✰ <b>6++ stars</b> ✰<br /><br />It’s ironic how, before I decided to pick up Law Man, I’ve been wanting to read KA books for some time but was intimidated because of the amount of books she has, not knowing where to start, but, now that I was able get a glimpse of her writing (<i>and absolutely loved it</i>), I’ve learned to appreciate that fact because it only means I have so much more books to look forward to - and it’s all thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/41864935-melissa" rel="nofollow noopener">Mel</a> for helping me where to start or I’d have been a lost cause lmaoo &lt;33<br /><br /><b>I didn’t need it. Because I wasn’t a Two Point Five. I wasn’t an Eight. I wasn’t a Ten. Mitch was right. My classification system was bullshit. Bottom line, what I was is a decent person. And I always had been.</b><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Mara (h):</b>
</u><br />lemme start with talking about my girl, Mara. I’ve adored a lot of heroines before, but there have been <i>very few</i> where I can say I genuinely related to and Mara is one of those few. Every thought she had, every decision she made - it’s something I see myself thinking/doing. The only differences between us was I didn’t have Mara World/her classification system (ngl this annoyed me a bit, but I also understood why she had these thoughts) and her heartbreaking past but everything else about her was basically who I am. What I loved the most about Mara tho was seeing her development throughout the book. I literally cried during the scene when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[she stood up to her mom and went off cause I was just so proud of her for finally realizing her worth!! 🤩💖 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>“But what I want you to know is that I’d like you to come over but because you’re shy, you gotta walk that breezeway, sweetheart. I’m tellin’ you you’re welcome but I made the first move, you need to make the next one. You with me here?”</b><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Mitch (H):</b>
</u><br />The name of this series actually makes sense cause Mitch was the definition of a dream man. Honestly tho, where can I find my own Mitch?? The way he never gave up on Mara, no matter how much she kept pushing him away; he has my respect. I can’t find a single flaw in him (call me whipped idc). He’s patient. He’s hilarious. He took Billie and Billy in as if they were his own, no questions asked. He’s swoon worthy. He’s straight forward. He’s just a good guy overall. <i>What more can one ask for?</i><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Billie/Billy:</b>
</u><br />These two were adorable af and they both deserved the world. Billy’s insecurities...man. My heart broke for him. He’s only a kid yet forced to grow up and have thoughts he shouldn’t have to deal with at his age, simply because of their shitty father. But I loved how much of a sunshine Billie was and she just has my heart. &lt;3<br /><br />Tbh I find the rest of the side characters (the good ones, I mean) to be likable as well! I loved reading Mitch and Mara’s interactions with each character, no matter how simple the scene may be. As for Mara’s mom and aunt, they’re both on my shit list. They were annoying and I was not amused at all whenever they would appear smh. I’m aware Tack’s book is next and I’m excited to read his story! ♡</span>
  <a data-text-id="6081309886809162689" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

She has fantasized about him, and been privately in love with him since the first time she experienced his magnificent smile. She watches him, and all the ladies coming and going, and wishes it was her in his bed.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/920c2d7a-b662-4313-aee4-1d00c1eb9a7e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer273666867" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17384293961522233209"><u>First read: March 19-20, 2012</u><br/><br/>What can I say that hasn't already been said about this book from those who have read it and LOVED it?<br/>I don't know what how Kristen Ashley does it, or how she can write so many 'great' stories about such awesome characters...but man I'm hooked!<br/><br/>I haven't read one book of hers that I haven't liked or loved for that matter!<br/>It's not that the stories are complex or brain-draining.. there just really good chick-lit, romantic, humorous, bone-wrenching stories with the ABSOL</span>
  <span id="freeText17384293961522233209" style="display:none"><u>First read: March 19-20, 2012</u><br /><br />What can I say that hasn't already been said about this book from those who have read it and LOVED it?<br />I don't know what how Kristen Ashley does it, or how she can write so many 'great' stories about such awesome characters...but man I'm hooked!<br /><br />I haven't read one book of hers that I haven't liked or loved for that matter!<br />It's not that the stories are complex or brain-draining.. there just really good chick-lit, romantic, humorous, bone-wrenching stories with the ABSOLUTE BEST Happily Ever Afters!<br /><br /><u>Favorite quote in the book:</u><br /><br /><i> -This excerpt is from Mara speaking to her Mother, her Aunt Lulamae, and Jez (Billie's biological mother) these people are fondly known as "The Trailer Trash Trio" (gotta love the names in this book *smile*) who's mission is to mess with Mara and bring her down a notch.<br /><br /> <b>"I said they're MY KIDS. And seeing as they're mine, I love them and they love me, I will exhaust myself, I will run myself ragged, I will bleed myself dry and I will do this to make sure they're safe, protected, and stay WITH ME".</b></i><br /><br />Again Ms. Ashely speaks about life, and it's not always easy but the rewards of it is safety, protection, and all of it done out of LOVE.....and it's a Beautiful Thing!<br /><br />Ms. Ashley's female leads are usually broken, but have an amazing strength that when it really matters they step-up and fight for what they believe in and then they SHINE!<br /><br />Loved this book, highly recommend it, and can't wait to read Tack's book!<br /><br /><br /><u>Second read: August 6-7, 2014</u><br /><br />Really enjoyed this re-read. <br />It has been a little over 2 years since I first read this story, and I was happy to discover that even though I 'kinda' remembered the story..it still wasn't fresh and I soon found myself caught up in the story and the characters.<br />LOVED IT!</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2388568892?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Just Josie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Just Josie" href="/user/show/5942176-just-josie">Just Josie</a>

        rated it
